		&lt;div id="oswald-bio" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="LHO oswald-bio LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop right"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Lee Harvey Oswald&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;Lee Harvey Oswald (born October 18, 1939) was the accused assassin of President John F. Kennedy. A former Marine, he was only 24 years old at the time of the shooting. During his youth, Lee studied Marxism and Communism as he tried to find his place in a society he rejected.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;div id="jfk-bio" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="JFK jfk-bio JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;John F. Kennedy&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;John Fitzgerald &ldquo;Jack&rdquo; Kennedy (born May 29, 1917) was the 35th president of the United States. At 43 years old, he was the youngest elected and first Roman Catholic president. At just 46, he was also the youngest to die in office.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

			&lt;h5&gt;Jack&rsquo;s Early Years&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
			
		&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-intro-jfk-a-location-identifier-b" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;
			&lt;h5&gt;Jack&rsquo;s Harvard Graduation&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
			
		&lt;div id="ambition-intro-jfk-a-young-aspirations" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-intro-jfk-a-young-aspirations JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Young Aspirations&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;Growing up, Jack enjoys a comfortable life filled with private schooling and summers at the family compound in Hyannis Port on Cape Cod in Massachusetts. His father, Joseph Kennedy Sr., encourages competition between his sons and expects the boys to succeed at everything.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		&lt;div id="ambition-intro-and-jfk-a-early-life-caption" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-intro-and-jfk-a-early-life-caption JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Jack&rsquo;s Collegiate Career&lt;/h3&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;As a Harvard University student like his father and brother before him, Jack befriends many of his professors and peers.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		&lt;a href="#!/ambition-intro-jfk-a-secondary/meet-the-kennedys"&gt;&lt;img data-default_parallax="40px 40px" id="meet-the-kennedys" data-default_parallax="15px 15px" class="meet-the-kennedys secondaryIcon" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/icon-jfk-red-image-shadow.png"/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

		&lt;div id="ambition-a-oswald-young-alienation" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-a-oswald-young-alienation LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop right"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Young Alienation&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;Before Lee is born, his father dies suddenly, the first event of many in a life plagued by abandonment and neglect. As his third birthday approaches, his mother, Marguerite Oswald, leaves her son at the Bethlehem Children&rsquo;s Home in New Orleans. Even though she brings him home 13 months later, Lee later believes she thinks of him as a burden. &lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		&lt;div id="ambition-a-lho-driven-to-drop-out-caption" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-a-lho-driven-to-drop-out-caption LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingF"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Driven to Drop Out&lt;/h3&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;Marguerite moves the family to New York in 1952, presumably to be closer to Lee&rsquo;s older brother John. Amidst constant battles with Lee&rsquo;s truancy and poor behavior, the Oswalds return to New Orleans in 1954 and Lee completes the ninth grade. He&rsquo;s back in school, but not for long.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-a-lho-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoOrange"&gt;
			&lt;h5&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Early Years&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-a-lho-location-identifier-b" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoGreen"&gt;
			&lt;h5&gt;Lee Drops Out&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		
		&lt;div id="ambition-a-lho-redOverlay" class="redQuoteBG fullComposition"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;

			&lt;cite&gt;JFK&lt;/cite&gt;

		&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-b-oswald-jfk-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;
			&lt;h5&gt;Jack Joins the Navy&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		
		&lt;img id="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-mapLeft" class="halfCompositionLeft" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/b/JFK/ambition-B-JFK-map-600x900.jpg"/&gt;
		
		&lt;img id="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-jfkLight" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-jfkLight" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/b/JFK/ambition-B-JFK-silo-656x845.png"/&gt;
		
		&lt;div id="ambition-b-oswald-jfk-called-to-serve" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-b-oswald-jfk-called-to-serve JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Called to Serve&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;Upon his Harvard commencement in 1940, Jack joins the Navy, is made lieutenant and is sent to captain the PT-109, a three-engine wooden patrol torpedo boat stationed near the Solomon Islands in the South Pacific during World War II.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		&lt;div id="ambition-b-jfk-oswald-called-to-serve" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-b-jfk-oswald-called-to-serve LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Called to Serve&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;October 18, 1956, marks Lees 17th birthday. Six days later he enlists in the Marine Corps. By the end of the month this high school dropout reports for duty at the Marine Corps Recruit Depot in San Diego, California.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		&lt;img id="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-bullet1" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-bullet1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/b/LHO/ambition-B-LHO-bullet1-68x68.png"/&gt;	
		&lt;img id="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-bullet2" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-bullet2" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/b/LHO/ambition-B-LHO-bullet2-58x57.png"/&gt;	
		&lt;img id="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-bullet3" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-bullet3" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/b/LHO/ambition-B-LHO-bullet3-57x62.png"/&gt;
		
		&lt;div id="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-LHO-sharpshooter-caption" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-b-jfk-and-lho-LHO-sharpshooter-caption LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Sharpshooter&lt;/h3&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;In 1956, Lee trains in the use of the M-1 rifle. While his practice scores are less than impressive, when his company fires for record on December 21, he scores 212two points above the score necessary to qualify as a &ldquo;sharpshooter&rdquo; on the marksman/expert scale. He is posted to the Atsugi Air Force Base in Japan.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-b-jfk-oswald-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoOrange"&gt;
			&lt;h5&gt;Lee Joins the Marine Corps&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;div id="ambition-c-oswald-map-asperations-of-allegiance" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-c-oswald-map-asperations-of-allegiance LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
				&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
				&lt;h3&gt;Aspirations of Allegiance&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
			&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
				&lt;p&gt;Lee&rsquo;s two courts-martial leave him disenchanted with both the Military and American life. He takes a renewed interest in the Socialism he idealized in his childhood and makes plans to travel to the Soviet Union. In August 1959, Lee claims he must care for his injured mother and is granted a three-month early discharge from the Marine Corps. He writes the USSR, requesting citizenship.&lt;/p&gt;
			&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		&lt;div id="ambition-c-oswald-map-citizenship-quote" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-c-oswald-map-citizenship-quote LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
			&lt;blockquote class="callOut"&gt;&ldquo;I want citizenship because I am a Communist and a worker; I have lived in a decadent capitalist society where the workers are slaves.&rdquo;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		
		&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-c-lho-map-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoOrange"&gt;
			&lt;h5&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Defection&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		
		
		&lt;a href="#!/ambition-c-oswald-map-secondary/good-bye-america"&gt;&lt;img id="good-bye-america" data-default_parallax="80px 80px" class="iconAudio secondaryIcon good-bye-america" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/icon-lho-gray-audio-shadow.png"/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;
    </script>
    <script id="section_ambition_c_lho_moscow_template" type="text/x-handlebars-template">

	&lt;div id="ambition-c-lho-moscow-suicide-caption" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="ambition-c-lho-moscow-suicide-caption LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Facing Death&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Soviet officials offer Lee little information and no encouragement concerning his application for citizenship. He is told to leave Moscow and responds by cutting open his left wrist. He recovers in a nearby hospital.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="ambition-c-lho-moscow-blackOverlay" class="blackBG fullComposition"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;


	&lt;img id="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-citizenship-revoked-letter" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-citizenship-revoked-letter" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/c/LHO/ambition-C-LHO-letter2-504x665.png"/&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-citizenship-revoked-letter-highlight" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" data-transform_origin="-32px -129px" class="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-citizenship-revoked-letter-highlight" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/c/LHO/ambition-C-LHO-letter2-highlight-403x92.jpg"/&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-citizenship-revoked-quote" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-citizenship-revoked-quote LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote class="callOut"&gt;&ldquo;I Lee Harvey Oswald do hereby request that my present citizenship in the United States of America, be revoked.&rdquo;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-c-oswald-moscow-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoOrange"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Lee in Moscow&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
    </script>
    <script id="section_ambition_c_jfk_political_career_template" type="text/x-handlebars-template">
     &lt;img id="ambition-c-jfk-political-career-bg-left" class="halfCompositionLeft" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/c/JFK/ambition-C-JFK-bg-left-600x900.jpg"/&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="ambition-c-jfk-political-career-bg-right" class="halfCompositionRight" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/01-ambition/c/JFK/ambition-C-JFK-bg-right-600x900.jpg"/&gt;

	&lt;div id="ambition-c-jfk-political-career-congress-caption" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="ambition-c-jfk-political-career-congress-caption JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Jack for Congressman&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On Election Day in 1946, Kennedy swamps his opponents in Massachusetts&rsquo;s 11th Congressional District after long-time Boston politico James Michael Curley vacates his seat.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-c-jfk-political-career-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Jack&rsquo;s Political Goals&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="ambition-d-jfk-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Jack&rsquo;s Presidential Hopes&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="ambition-lockup-LHO-caption" class="LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionLeft responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingF"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Sent to Work in Minsk&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Lee is summoned to the Soviet passport office on January 4, 1960. He is hopeful he will attend Moscow University. However, Lee is given an Identity Document for Stateless Persons and is shipped 450 miles southwest to the industrial city of Minsk.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="ambition-lockup-JFK-caption" class="JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionRight responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Jack&rsquo;s Inauguration &lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On a chilly January 20, 1961, John F. Kennedy is sworn in as the 35th President of the United States of America.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;img id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-letter2-bottom" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-letter2-bottom" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/LHO/failure-A-LHO-letter2-bottom-499x316.png"/&gt;
	&lt;img id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-letter2-top" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-letter2-top" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/LHO/failure-A-LHO-letter2-top-499x316.png"/&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-letter1-bottom" data-default_parallax="50px 50px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-letter1-bottom" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/LHO/failure-A-LHO-letter1-bottom-498x341.png"/&gt;

	&lt;img id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-envelope" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-envelope" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/LHO/failure-A-LHO-envelope-551x430.png"/&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-quote" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-quote LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote class="callOut"&gt;&ldquo;&hellip;we shall recive (sic) our visa&rsquo;s (sic) about the middle of February, which means we may arrive in the U.S. about the 1st of March give or take a month or so.&rdquo;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-lees-letter-home" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-lees-letter-home LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingE"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Letters Home&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Lee writes Marguerite often while in the USSR. In one of his final letters, he tells his mother of his upcoming return to the United States. Lee&rsquo;s experiment with Communism has failed.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	
	&lt;img id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-polaroid" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-polaroid" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/LHO/failure-A-LHO-polaroid-463x593.png"/&gt;
	&lt;div id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-lee-looks-to-america" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-lee-looks-to-america LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee Looks To America&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;After a year in Minsk, Lee is already giving up on his new life&mdash;the Soviet Union is no place for a young man seeking independence. He contacts the American Embassy and informs them of one sure thing&mdash;he wants to go home. Paperwork and red tape force him to wait more than a year to take his new wife and child to America.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	
	&lt;img id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-discharge" data-default_parallax="50px 50px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-discharge" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/LHO/failure-A-LHO-discharge-795x921.png"/&gt;
	
	
	&lt;div id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-undesirable-discharge" data-default_parallax="40px 40px" class="failure-intro-and-lho-a-undesirable-discharge LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingG"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee is Undesirably Discharged&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;When Lee defects to the Soviet Union, he has inactive status in the Marine Corps Reserve, following his requested transfer from active duty. When the Reserve learns of his defection, he is undesirably discharged. &lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-intro-a-poem" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="poem failure-intro-a-poem responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote&gt;But I&rsquo;ve a rendezvous with Death&lt;br&gt;At midnight in some flaming town,&lt;/blockquote&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="failure-intro-and-lho-a-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoOrange"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Life in Minsk&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;


	&lt;img id="failure-intro-a-chapter-twotitle" data-default_parallax="60px 60px" class="failure-intro-a-chapter-twotitle" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/intro/ambition-intro-chaptertitle-98x14.png"/&gt;

	&lt;img id="failure-A-JFK-castro-556x575" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="failure-A-JFK-castro-556x575" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/JFK/failure-A-JFK-castro-556x575.png"/&gt;

	&lt;div id="failure-A-JFK-foreground-communism-on-the-rise" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="failure-A-JFK-foreground-communism-on-the-rise JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Communism on the Rise&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;It&rsquo;s a new decade, yet fear of the global spread of Communism is still alive in America. Castro makes a deal with the Soviets to trade Cuban sugar in exchange for Soviet oil, placing him at the center of a dangerous power struggle between the U.S. and the Soviet Union. Castro has turned this small island into his own personal soapbox.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;


	&lt;div id="failure-A-JFK-foreground-fidel-castro-bio" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="failure-A-JFK-foreground-fidel-castro-bio JFK contentContainer JFK-contentContainer bio responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
		&lt;img src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/JFK/failure-A-JFK-FidelBio.jpg" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/a/JFK/failure-A-JFK-FidelBio.jpg"/&gt;
		&lt;div class="caption"&gt;
			&lt;img class="medallion" src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/medallion-castro-aqua.png" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/medallion-castro-aqua.png"/&gt;
			&lt;h4&gt;Fidel Castro&lt;/h4&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="description"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Fidel Castro (born August 13, 1926) led the overthrow of Cuba&rsquo;s dictator in 1959, then maneuvered himself into the same role as head of the new government and made Cuba the first Communist country in the Western Hemisphere. During his long reign, thousands of Cubans fled to the U.S.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="failure-A-JFK-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Cuba&rsquo;s Political Climate&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
    </script>
    <script id="section_failure_jfk_b_cuba_quote_template" type="text/x-handlebars-template">
     &lt;img id="failure-B-JFK-quote-bg-left-600x900" class="halfCompositionLeft" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/b/JFK/failure-B-JFK-quote-bg-left-600x900.jpg"/&gt;
	&lt;img id="failure-B-JFK-quote-bg-right-600x900" class="halfCompositionRight" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/b/JFK/failure-B-JFK-quote-bg-right-600x900.jpg"/&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-B-JFK-quote-quote" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="failure-B-JFK-quote-quote JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote class="fontStyleNormal"&gt;&ldquo;Let every nation know, whether it wishes us well or ill, that we shall pay any price, bear any burden, meet any hardship, support any friend, oppose any foe to assure the survival and the success of liberty.&rdquo;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
		&lt;cite&gt;JFK&lt;/cite&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

    <script id="section_failure_jfk_c_cuba_template" type="text/x-handlebars-template">

	&lt;div id="failure-C-JFK-allen-dulles-bio" data-default_parallax="60px 60px" class="failure-C-JFK-allen-dulles-bio JFK JFK-contentContainer bio contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;img src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/c/JFK/failure-C-JFK-AllenDulles.jpg" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/c/JFK/failure-C-JFK-AllenDulles.jpg"/&gt;

			&lt;img class="medallion" src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/medallion-dulles-aqua.png" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/medallion-dulles-aqua.png"/&gt;
			&lt;h4&gt;Allen Dulles&lt;/h4&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="description"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Allen Dulles (born April 7, 1893) was the deputy director of the Central Intelligence Agency from 1953 to 1961, during the darkest days of the cold war. Appointed by President Eisenhower, Dulles&rsquo;s time was spent combating Communist expansion and influence worldwide through low-cost espionage rather than massive spending on conventional U.S. military forces. &lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="failure-C-JFK-preStrike-624x424" data-default_parallax="45px 45px"class="failure-C-JFK-preStrike-624x424" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/c/JFK/failure-C-JFK-preStrike-624x424.png"/&gt;
	&lt;img id="failure-C-JFK-postStrike-598x413" data-default_parallax="50px 50px" class="failure-C-JFK-postStrike-598x413" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/c/JFK/failure-C-JFK-postStrike-598x413.png"/&gt;
	
	
	&lt;div id="failure-C-JFK-conquering-communism" data-default_parallax="60px 60px" class="failure-C-JFK-conquering-communism JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Conquering Communism&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Only weeks after Jack takes office, the CIA chief discusses the details of a secret U.S. plan to send Cuban exiles back to their homeland to overthrow the very man they&rsquo;ve fled: Fidel Castro.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="failure-C-JFK-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Bay of Pigs Crisis&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
    </script>
    <script id="section_failure_jfk_d_bay_of_pigs_template" type="text/x-handlebars-template">
     &lt;img id="failure-D-JFK-bop-background-left-600x900" class="halfCompositionLeft" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/d/JFK/failure-D-JFK-bop-background-left-600x900.jpg"/&gt;
	&lt;img id="failure-D-JFK-bop-background-right-600x900" class="halfCompositionRight" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/d/JFK/failure-D-JFK-bop-background-right-600x900.jpg"/&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="failure-D-JFK-bop-foreground-225x676" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="failure-D-JFK-bop-foreground-225x676" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/02-failure/d/JFK/failure-D-JFK-bop-foreground-260x688.png"/&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-D-JFK-bop-bay-of-pigs-blunders" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="failure-D-JFK-bop-bay-of-pigs-blunders JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Blunders in the Bay&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;A series of missteps and misfortunes is the plan&rsquo;s rapid undoing. Jack puts a stop to air cover, fearful of revealing U.S. involvement in the attack. The Cuban exiles&rsquo; landing site is a mosquito-ridden swamp, miles from the refuge of the mountains. And miscommunication over the timing causes a secondary air mission to fail.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-D-JFK-bop-bay-of-pigs" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="failure-D-JFK-bop-bay-of-pigs JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Exiles Invade&lt;br /&gt;Their Homeland&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Though Jack wishes to keep U.S. involvement under wraps, he gives the go-ahead for 1,400 Cuban exiles to launch an invasion at the Bay of Pigs on the southern coast of Cuba. They are immediately met with heavy fire. &lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-jfk-d-bay-of-pigs-redOverlay" class="redQuoteBG fullComposition"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-jfk-d-bay-of-pigs-quote-jfk" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="failure-jfk-e-bay-of-pigs-quote-quote JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote class="fontStyleNormal"&gt;&ldquo;I don't want the United States involved in this.&rdquo;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
		&lt;cite&gt;JFK&lt;/cite&gt;

		&lt;blockquote class="fontStyleNormal"&gt;&ldquo;Hell, Mr. President, we are involved.&rdquo;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
		&lt;cite&gt;Admiral Arleigh Burke&lt;/cite&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="failure-jfk-d-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkRed"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Bay of Pigs Crisis&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
    </script>

		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;LBJ vs. Bobby&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;An already contentious relationship between the vice president and the attorney general is further strained as a consequence of the Bay of Pigs fiasco. Jack calls Bobby, not LBJ, into the Oval Office to confide in him his fear of failure. This is the beginning of what some will call Bobby&rsquo;s role as assistant president.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Disillusions of Grandeur&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In mid-May 1962, the Oswald family leaves Minsk to begin their journey to the United States. They arrive on June 13.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="failure-lockup-JFK-caption" class="JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionRight responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;The Coup Collapses&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On the evening of April 19, 1961, Cuban forces have total control of the Bay of Pigs. The invasion fails&mdash;1,189 are captured, 114 killed.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;blockquote&gt;It may be he shall take my hand&lt;br&gt;And lead me into his dark land&lt;br&gt;And close my eyes and quench my breath&lt;br&gt;It may be I shall pass him still.&lt;/blockquote&gt;

	&lt;div id="adversity-intro-and-lho-dallas-unnoticed" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="adversity-intro-and-lho-dallas-unnoticed LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingG"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Going Unnoticed in Texas&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Lee is disappointed with the lackluster welcome he receives at Love Field Airport in Dallas. He soon learns his return is being more closely tracked than he could imagine.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="adversity-jfk-a-CMC-begins" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="adversity-jfk-a-CMC-begins JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;The Cuban Missile Crisis Begins&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Overnight, American pilots photograph the installation of Soviet ballistic missiles in Cuba. CIA analysts quickly identify several newly established missile bases within 100 miles of the U.S. On October 16, Jack is briefed on the situation as the world tips frighteningly close to nuclear war.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;a href="#!/adversity-jfk-a-CMC/adversity-jfk-a-CMC-sec1"&gt;&lt;img id="adversity-jfk-a-CMC-sec1" class="secondaryIcon adversity-jfk-a-CMC-sec1" data-default_parallax="75px 75px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/medallion-krushchev-cream-small-shadow.png"/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="adversity-A-JFK-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkRed"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Jack &amp; Cuba&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
    </script>

		&lt;cite&gt;JFK&lt;/cite&gt;

	&lt;/div&gt;


	&lt;div id="adversity-lockup-LHO-caption" class="LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionLeft responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee Goes to Louisiana&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;After losing his job and having difficulty finding work, Marina suggests Lee move to New Orleans, his birthplace. On August 24, 1963, Lee leaves Dallas, and Marina and June, behind for now. His family joins him as soon as he finds a job and secures an apartment. Once settled in New Orleans however, Lee&rsquo;s struggles continue as he tries to find his place.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="adversity-lockup-JFK-caption" class="JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionRight responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;The Height of the Crisis&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On October 22, Jack reveals the crisis to the world and calls for the missiles&rsquo; removal. Over the past six days, the Kennedy brothers have resisted pressure from the military to bomb the missile sites. Jack declares a naval blockade of Cuba, giving the Soviet Union the opportunity to dismantle and withdraw peacefully. The nation braces itself for a possible nuclear war.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="adversity-lockup-instructions" class="lockup-instructions" data-lockup_parallax="750px 20px" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/tilt-laptop.png"/&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;The Kennedy Children&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;During Jack&rsquo;s presidency, Caroline and John Jr. often visit him in the Oval Office.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="loveloss-A-LHO-familyBg-left-600x900" class="halfCompositionLeft" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/04-loveloss/a/LHO/loveloss-A-LHO-familyBg-left-600x900.jpg"/&gt;

	&lt;div id="loveloss-intro-poem" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="poem loveloss-intro-poem responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote&gt;God knows &rsquo;twere better to be deep&lt;br&gt;Pillowed in silk and scented down,&lt;br&gt;Where love throbs out in blissful sleep,&lt;br&gt;Pulse nigh to pulse, and breath to breath,&lt;br&gt;Where hushed awakenings are dear&hellip;&lt;/blockquote&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	

	
	&lt;img id="loveloss-intro-chaptertitle-99x15" data-default_parallax="60px 60px" class="loveloss-intro-chaptertitle-99x15" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/04-loveloss/intro/loveloss-intro-chaptertitle-99x15.png"/&gt;

	&lt;img id="loveloss-intro-loss-245x60" data-default_parallax="65px 65px" class="loveloss-intro-loss-245x60" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/04-loveloss/intro/loveloss-intro-loss-245x60.png"/&gt;
	
	
	
	&lt;div id="loveloss-intro-lee-and-marina-caption" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="loveloss-intro-lee-and-marina-caption LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingD"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;International Love&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Lee meets Marina in March 1961 and is immediately smitten. He enters the hospital soon after for an adenoid operation and Marina visits him constantly.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	
	
	&lt;div id="loveloss-intro-royal-family-caption" data-default_parallax="35px 35px" class="loveloss-intro-royal-family-caption JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;America&rsquo;s Royal Family&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Jack cherishes his wife and is a doting father. The couple&rsquo;s beauty, youth and glamour enchant the public at home and abroad. By the second year of Jack&rsquo;s presidency, the Kennedys are referred to as &ldquo;America&lsquo;s Royal Family.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;img id="loveloss-A-JFK-polaroid-444x567" data-default_parallax="45px 45px" class="loveloss-A-JFK-polaroid-444x567" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/04-loveloss/a/JFK/loveloss-A-JFK-polaroid-444x567.png"/&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="loveloss-intro-to-have-to-hold" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="loveloss-intro-to-have-to-hold LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop left cf"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;To Have and to Hold&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Less than two months after they meet, Lee and Marina wed on April 30, 1961, in Minsk.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="loveloss-intro-until-death" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="loveloss-intro-until-death JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop right cf"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Until Death Do Us Part&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;When Jack is a congressman, he meets and proposes to Jacqueline Bouvier, a young reporter. The couple marries on September 12, 1953, shortly before Jack is elected to the Senate.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="loveloss-intro-born-out-of-love" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="loveloss-intro-born-out-of-love LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop left cf"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Born Out of Love&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Marina becomes pregnant soon after the couple weds. June Lee Oswald is born February 15, 1962, in Minsk. Lee is excited but does not see the baby until Marina leaves the hospital eight days later, in accordance with local customs. Their second daughter, Audrey Rachel Lee, is born on October 20, 1963, at Parkland Hospital in Dallas, Texas.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
					
	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="loveloss-intro-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoOrange"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Lee Marries in Minsk&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="loveloss-intro-location-identifier-b" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkRed"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Jack Weds in Rhode Island&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="loveloss-intro-location-identifier-c" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Rough Waters to the U.S.&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In 1962 Marina leaves Minsk with Lee and June. While on the SS Maasdam en route to the U.S., Marina notices that Lee is nervous and spends a great deal of time by himself in the library. He pays Marina little attention, acting ashamed of her. Her troubles, however, are only beginning.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="loveloss-B-LHO-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoGreen"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Lee Overlooks Marina&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;a href="#!/loveloss-lho-b-secondary/loveloss-lho-b-secondary-sec1"&gt;&lt;img id="loveloss-lho-b-secondary-sec1" data-default_parallax="70px 70px" class="secondaryIcon loveloss-lho-b-secondary-sec1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/icon-lho-orange-info-shadow.png"/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Political Affairs&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Marilyn Monroe, one of Jack&rsquo;s extramarital interests, at a democratic fundraising birthday party for the president in New York.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="loveloss-jfk-b-secondary-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkBlue"&gt;

	&lt;div id="loveloss-lockup-LHO-caption" class="LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionLeft responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingC"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee on His Own&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Back in Dallas, Marina notices how isolated and calculating Lee is becoming. She realizes his interest in politics&mdash;and guns&mdash;is growing and he is willing to act on his ideas.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="loveloss-lockup-JFK-caption" class="JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionRight responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Heartbreak and Happiness&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On August 7, 1963, almost six weeks early, Jackie is rushed to Otis Air Force Base, where she delivers Patrick Bouvier Kennedy. The premature baby is born with lung deficiencies and is rushed to Children&rsquo;s Hospital in Boston before Jackie is even able to hold her newborn son.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="conviction-intro-poem" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="poem conviction-intro-poem responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote&gt;I have a rendezvous with Death&lt;br/&gt;On some scarred slope of battered hill,&lt;br/&gt;When Spring comes round again this year&lt;br&gt;And the first meadow-flowers appear.&lt;/blockquote&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Black and White Issues&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In the 1960s, the civil rights movement peaks as spontaneous sit-ins and so-called &ldquo;Freedom Riders&rdquo; aim to break down segregated buses, restaurants and waiting rooms. The protests are peaceful, but are often met with violent force that&rsquo;s televised and helps win the support of sympathetic whites in the North. The Kennedy brothers decide to act.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
			
	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="conviction-intro-and-a-jfk-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier jfkRed"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Jack &amp; Civil Rights&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Who Is A.J. Hidell?&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In 1963, Lee carries business cards with the alias &ldquo;A.J. Hidell,&rdquo; the president of the Fair Play for Cuba Committee in New Orleans. He uses the same alias to purchase two guns.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="conviction-lockup-LHO-caption" class="LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionLeft responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Shooting Lee&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In the early spring, Lee makes Marina photograph him with his new rifle and pistol. He also holds two popular Socialist newspapers, &lt;italic&gt;The Worker&lt;/italic&gt; and &lt;italic&gt;The Militant&lt;/italic&gt;. &lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="conviction-lockup-JFK-caption" class="JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionRight responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;The March on Washington&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In August, more than 250,000 Americans of all races and backgrounds join in the March on Washington for Jobs and Freedom. Key civil rights leaders spearhead the march, addressing the crowds from the steps of the Lincoln Memorial. The most memorable of those is the Reverend Dr. Martin Luther King Jr. delivering a speech named &ldquo;I Have a Dream.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="fate-intro-taking-on-texas" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="fate-intro-taking-on-texas JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Taking on Texas&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Jack&rsquo;s visit to Texas is a strategic onehe needs to improve his political fortune and popularity in this pivotal state he barely carried in 1960. His two-day schedule is filled with public appearances, which Jack always personally enjoyed.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	

	&lt;div id="fate-intro-blackOverlayFull" class="blackBG fullComposition"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="fate-intro-poem" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="poem fate-intro-poem responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote&gt;And I to my pledged word am true,&lt;br&gt;I shall not fail that rendezvous.&lt;/blockquote&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;


	&lt;img id="fate-intro-chaptertitle-99x14" data-default_parallax="60px 60px" class="fate-intro-chaptertitle-99x14" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/06-fate/intro/fate-intro-chaptertitle-99x14.png"/&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Left Alone&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Bonnie Ray Williams, a School Book Depository sixth-floor employee, eats lunch then goes to the fifth floor to watch the motorcade with friends. Lee is alone on the sixth floor.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="fate-lho-b-job-lee-finds-work" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="fate-lho-b-job-lee-finds-work LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf left"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;A New Job in Dallas&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;In October 1963, Lee begins working at the Texas School Book Depository in downtown Dallas.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div data-default_parallax="0px 0px" id="fate-lho-b-location-identifier-a" class="responsiveToCenterSectionContainer locationIdentifier lhoGreen"&gt;
		&lt;h5&gt;Lee Finds Work&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;a href="#!/fate-lho-b-job-secondary/fate-lho-b-job-secondary-LHO-sec1"&gt;&lt;img id="fate-lho-b-job-secondary-LHO-sec1" data-default_parallax="70px 70px" class="secondaryIcon fate-lho-b-job-secondary-LHO-sec1" src="data:image/gif;base64,R0lGODlhAQABAIAAAAAAAP///yH5BAEAAAAALAAAAAABAAEAAAIBRAA7" data-img_src="http://cdn1.killinglincoln.nationalgeographic.com/kennedy/1398428073/assets/global/icon-lho-green-image-shadow.png"/&gt;&lt;/a&gt;

	&lt;div id="fate-jfk-b-trip-dotes-on-jack" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="fate-jfk-b-trip-dotes-on-jack JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Dallas Dotes on Jack&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;As the motorcade is met by roaring crowds as it rolls through downtown, the governor's wife tells Jack, &ldquo;Mr. President, you can&rsquo;t say Dallas doesn't love you.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;		

	&lt;div id="fate-jfk-b-trip-jackie-spotlight" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="fate-jfk-b-trip-jackie-spotlight JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingA"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectTop cf right"&gt;
			&lt;span class="medallion"&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Jackie Steals the Spotlight&lt;/h3&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRectBottom"&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;As Jackie had not accompanied Jack on many of his trips, she receives as warm a welcome as he did in Texas. The morning of November 22, Jack recounted that two years ago in Europe he introduced himself as &ldquo;the man who had accompanied Mrs. Kennedy to Paris.&rdquo; He continued saying &ldquo;I get somewhat that same sensation as I travel around Texas. Nobody wonders what Lyndon and I wear.&rdquo;&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

		&lt;h5&gt;Day Two in Texas&lt;span&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/h5&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee&rsquo;s Escape Route&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;Lee hastily enters his building at around 1 p.m. and stays for  a few moments to grab his revolver from his room.&lt;/p&gt;

		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;The Final Last Rites&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;At Parkland Hospital, two priests administer Last Rites to Jack. This is the fourth and final time a priest recites these words of faith to Jack.&lt;/p&gt;

	&lt;div id="fate-laid-to-rest-lockup-LHO-caption" class="LHO LHO-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionLeft responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectLeft"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Lee Is Laid to Rest&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On November 25, 1963, Lee is buried in Fort Worth. Close family and reporters are among the small number of attendees.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="fate-laid-to-rest-lockup-JFK-caption" class="JFK JFK-contentContainer contentContainer lockupCaptionRight responsiveToCenterSectionContainer pairingB"&gt;
		&lt;div class="roundedRect roundedRectRight"&gt;
			&lt;h3&gt;Jack Is Laid to Rest&lt;/h3&gt;
			&lt;p&gt;On November 25, 1963, Jack is buried in Arlington National Cemetery. It is a national day of mourning and nearly 800,000 Americans line the streets to watch the funeral procession from the Capitol to St. Matthew&rsquo;s Cathedral.&lt;/p&gt;
		&lt;/div&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;

	&lt;div id="fate-laid-to-rest-blackOverlay" class="blackBG fullComposition"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="fate-laid-to-rest-fact" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="poem responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote&gt;The events surrounding the JFK assassination left seven children fatherless in Dallas, Texas. Three women became widows. Two men with seemingly nothing in common were linked indefinitely. And one nation was forever changed.&lt;/blockquote&gt;
	&lt;/div&gt;
	
	&lt;div id="fate-laid-to-rest-poem" data-default_parallax="55px 55px" class="poem responsiveToCenterSectionContainer"&gt;
		&lt;blockquote&gt;And I to my pledged word am true&hellip;&lt;br&gt;I shall not fail that rendezvous.&lt;/blockquote&gt;
